### Example 1
Rule:
You can pick-up color1. You can stack color1 on-top-of color2. You can stack color1 on-top-of table.

<yellow>
<blue on green>

Goal state:

<yellow on blue on green>

step 1: pick-up yellow
step 2: stack yellow on-top-of blue
